{"id":"a1731020-a00c-42a0-bca9-35da9eeb8748","identifier":"FRG-223","title":"Agent-to-Agent Handshaking (Talk Protocol)","description":"Character-to-character interaction needs a request/response protocol instead of forced interaction.

## Current Problem

Talk is fire-and-forget: Character A decides to talk to B, walks over, and speaks — regardless of B's state. B could be sleeping, interacting with an object, or already talking to someone else.

## Requirements

1. **Request Phase:** When A decides to talk to B, A sends an interaction request.
2. **Evaluate Phase:** B checks current priority/state:
   * If idle or walking → Accept
   * If sleeping, interacting, or already in conversation → Reject
3. **Synchronization:** If accepted, both enter a shared 'talking' state. Both face each other. Individual AI decision timers pause until conversation ends.
4. **Conversation Duration:** Configurable (e.g., 10-15s), then both return to idle.
5. **Rejection Handling:** If B rejects, A falls back to alternative action (see fallback ticket).

## Acceptance Criteria

* Characters don't talk to sleeping/busy characters
* Both characters visibly enter conversation state
* Decision timers pause during conversation

USERMESSAGE #17
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→  }
   152→
   153→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   154→
   155→  get px() {
   156→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   157→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   158→    }
   159→    const next = this.path[0];
   160→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   161→  }
   162→
   163→  get py() {
   164→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   165→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   166→    }
   167→    const next = this.path[0];
   168→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   169→  }
   170→
   171→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   172→
   173→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   174→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   175→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   176→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   177→
   178→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   179→      this.path         = path;
   180→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   181→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   182→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   183→      this.action       = 'walking';
   184→
   185→      // Set initial facing from first step
   186→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   187→      this._playWalkAnim();
   188→      return true;
   189→    }
   190→    return false;
   191→  }
   192→
   193→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   194→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   195→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   196→  }
   197→
   198→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   199→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   200→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   201→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   202→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   203→    if (this.sprite) {
   204→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   205→    }
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   209→
   210→  update(deltaMs) {
   211→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   212→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   213→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   214→
   215→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   216→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   217→
   218→      // Advance tiles
   219→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   220→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   221→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   222→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   223→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   224→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   225→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   226→      }
   227→
   228→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   229→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   230→        this.action       = 'idle';
   231→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   232→        this._playAnim('idle');
   233→      } else {
   234→        this._playWalkAnim();
   235→      }
   236→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   237→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   238→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   239→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   240→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   241→        this.action        = 'idle';
   242→        this.interactTarget = null;
   243→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   244→        this._playAnim('idle');
   245→      }
   246→    }
   247→
   248→    // Tick dialogue
   249→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   250→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   251→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   252→    }
   253→
   254→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   255→    if (this.sprite) {
   256→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   257→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   258→    }
   259→
   260→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   261→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   262→    }
   263→  }
   264→
   265→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   268→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   269→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   270→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   271→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   272→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   273→    });
   274→  }
   275→
   276→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   277→
   278→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   279→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   280→    const next = this.path[0];
   281→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   282→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   283→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   284→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   285→    } else {
   286→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   287→    }
   288→  }
   289→
   290→  _playAnim(type) {
   291→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   292→    const key = type === 'idle'
   293→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   294→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   295→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   296→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   297→    }
   298→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   299→  }
   300→
   301→  _playWalkAnim() {
   302→    this._playAnim('walk');
   303→  }
   304→}
   305→

     1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object; let the
    54→      // timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => {
    77→          const slot = o.getSlotInfo();
    78→          return {
    79→            id:        o.id,
    80→            label:     o.label,
    81→            state:     o.state,
    82→            slots:     `${slot.available}/${slot.capacity} available`,
    83→            available: slot.available > 0,
    84→          };
    85→        });
    86→
    87→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    88→        .filter(c => {
    89→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    90→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    91→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
    92→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    93→        })
    94→        .map(c => ({ label: c.label, tx: Math.round(c.tx), ty: Math.round(c.ty), action: c.action }));
    95→
    96→      const systemPrompt =
    97→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
    98→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
    99→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
   100→
   101→      const userPrompt =
   102→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
   103→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
   104→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
   105→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
   106→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
   107→        `Choose one action:
` +
   108→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   109→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   110→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   111→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_label", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }`;
   112→
   113→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   114→
   115→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   116→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   117→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   118→        model: this.model,
   119→        max_tokens: 256,
   120→        system: systemPrompt,
   121→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   122→      });
   123→
   124→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   125→
   126→      if (!res.ok) {
   127→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   128→        return;
   129→      }
   130→
   131→      const data = await res.json();
   132→
   133→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   134→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   135→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   136→              ?? null;
   137→
   138→      if (!text) {
   139→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   140→        return;
   141→      }
   142→
   143→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   144→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   145→    } catch (err) {
   146→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   147→    } finally {
   148→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   149→    }
   150→  }
   151→
   152→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   153→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   154→
   155→    switch (decision.action) {
   156→      case 'move':
   157→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   158→          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely
   159→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   160→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   161→            if (prevObj) prevObj.release(character.name);
   162→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   163→          }
   164→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   165→        }
   166→        break;
   167→
   168→      case 'interact': {
   169→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   170→        if (obj) {
   171→          // If already heading to a different object, release that reservation first
   172→          if (character.targetObjectId && character.targetObjectId !== obj.id) {
   173→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   174→            if (prevObj) prevObj.release(character.name);
   175→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   176→          }
   177→
   178→          // Only commit if a slot is available
   179→          if (!obj.isFull()) {
   180→            // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   181→            const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   182→            if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   183→              obj.reserve(character.name); // claim slot before walking
   184→              character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   185→              character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   186→            }
   187→          }
   188→        }
   189→        break;
   190→      }
   191→
   192→      case 'idle':
   193→        // Release any pending reservation, then stay put for one full decision interval
   194→        if (character.targetObjectId) {
   195→          const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   196→          if (prevObj) prevObj.release(character.name);
   197→          character.targetObjectId = null;
   198→        }
   199→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   200→        break;
   201→
   202→      case 'talk': {
   203→        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);
   204→        if (target) {
   205→          // Walk Character A to a tile adjacent to Character B
   206→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   207→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   208→            // Initiator says something via speech bubble
   209→            if (decision.dialogue) {
   210→              character.pendingSpeech = decision.dialogue;
   211→            }
   212→            // Character B responds
   213→            if (decision.targetDialogue) {
   214→              target.pendingSpeech = decision.targetDialogue;
   215→            }
   216→            // Queue conversation event for the debug log
   217→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   218→              simState.pushEvent({
   219→                type: 'conversation',
   220→                speakerLabel: character.label,
   221→                targetLabel: target.label,
   222→                dialogue: decision.dialogue || '',
   223→                response: decision.targetDialogue || '',
   224→              });
   225→            }
   226→          }
   227→        }
   228→        break;
   229→      }
   230→    }
   231→
   232→    if (decision.dialogue) {
   233→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   234→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   235→    }
   236→
   237→    if (decision.description) {
   238→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   239→    }
   240→
   241→    if (this.onDecision) {
   242→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   243→    }
   244→  }
   245→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    67→      const prevAction        = char.action;
    68→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    69→
    70→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    72→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    76→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    77→        this._doWander(char);
    78→      }
    79→
    80→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    81→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    82→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    83→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    84→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    85→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
    86→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
    87→        }
    88→      }
    89→
    90→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
    91→      char.update(deltaMs);
    92→
    93→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
    94→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
    95→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
    96→      }
    97→    }
    98→  }
    99→
   100→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   101→
   102→  /**
   103→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   104→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   105→   */
   106→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   107→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   108→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   109→
   110→    if (event) {
   111→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   112→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   113→
   114→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   115→
   116→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   117→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   118→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   119→      if (obj && event.state) {
   120→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   121→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   122→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   123→        }
   124→      }
   125→
   126→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs);
   127→
   128→      if (event.speech) {
   129→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   130→      }
   131→
   132→      if (event.emoji) {
   133→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   134→      }
   135→    } else {
   136→      // No valid transition — release the reservation
   137→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   138→    }
   139→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   140→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   141→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   142→  }
   143→
   144→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   145→
   146→  _doWander(char) {
   147→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   148→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   149→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   150→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   151→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   152→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   153→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   154→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   155→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   156→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   157→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   158→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   159→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   160→            return;
   161→          }
   162→        }
   163→        // All objects full or unreachable — fall through to random wander
   164→      }
   165→    }
   166→
   167→    // Random walkable tile
   168→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   169→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   170→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   171→      return;
   172→    }
   173→
   174→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   175→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   176→
   177→    let moved = false;
   178→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   179→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   180→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   181→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   182→      if (moved) break;
   183→    }
   184→
   185→    if (!moved) {
   186→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   187→    }
   188→  }
   189→
   190→  /**
   191→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   192→   */
   193→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   194→    const dirs = [
   195→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   196→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   197→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   198→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   199→    ];
   200→    for (const d of dirs) {
   201→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   202→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   203→      }
   204→    }
   205→    return null;
   206→  }
   207→
   208→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   209→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   210→    const tiles = [];
   211→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   212→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   213→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   214→      }
   215→    }
   216→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   217→    return tiles;
   218→  }
   219→
   220→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   221→
   222→  getSimTimeString() {
   223→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   224→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   225→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   226→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   227→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   228→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   229→  }
   230→}

   261→    import { SimulationEngine } from './src/Engine.js';
   262→    import { Character } from './src/Character.js';
   263→    import { AIEngine } from './src/AIEngine.js';
   264→
   265→    // ── Walkable grid (mirrors scene.js) ──────────────────────────────────────
   266→
   267→    const GRID_COLS = 19;
   268→    const GRID_ROWS = 13;
   269→
   270→    function buildWalkableGrid() {
   271→      const grid = [];
   272→      for (let row = 0; row < GRID_ROWS; row++) {
   273→        const r = [];
   274→        for (let col = 0; col < GRID_COLS; col++) {
   275→          r.push(col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9);
   276→        }
   277→        grid.push(r);
   278→      }
   279→      // Mark tiles occupied by objects as non-walkable
   280→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   281→        const { tx, ty } = def.position;
   282→        if (ty >= 0 && ty < GRID_ROWS && tx >= 0 && tx < GRID_COLS) {
   283→          grid[ty][tx] = false;
   284→        }
   285→      }
   286→      return grid;
   287→    }
   288→
   289→    // ── Character definitions (mirrors scene.js) ─────────────────────────────
   290→
   291→    const CHARS_CONFIG = [
   292→      { name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 6,  ty: 7,
   293→        dialogue: ['Perfect brew today~', 'Want some tea?'] },
   294→      { name: 'Lucy',   label: 'Sol',   tx: 10, ty: 6,
   295→        dialogue: ['The bonsai looks healthy', 'Such peaceful light...'] },
   296→      { name: 'Ash',    label: 'Nyx',   tx: 13, ty: 5,
   297→        dialogue: ['I need more paint...', 'This light is perfect'] },
   298→    ];
   299→
   300→    // ── Engine setup ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   301→
   302→    const walkable = buildWalkableGrid();
   303→
   304→    const aiEngine = new AIEngine({
   305→      endpoint: '/api/llm',
   306→      model: 'anthropic/claude-3-haiku',
   307→      decisionIntervalMs: 30_000,
   308→      onDecision: (char, decision, objects) => {
   309→        const targetName = decision.targetId
   310→          ? (objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId)?.name ?? decision.targetId)
   311→          : decision.targetTile
   312→            ? `(${decision.targetTile.tx},${decision.targetTile.ty})`
   313→            : decision.targetCharacter
   314→              ?? null;
   315→        pushAILog(char.label, decision.action, targetName, decision.dialogue);
   316→      },
   317→    });
   318→
   319→    const simEngine = new SimulationEngine({ walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS, aiEngine });
   320→
   321→    for (const cfg of CHARS_CONFIG) {
   322→      simEngine.addCharacter(new Character({
   323→        ...cfg, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS,
   324→      }));
   325→    }
   326→
   327→    // ── UI state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   328→
   329→    let paused = false;
   330→    let speed  = 1;
   331→    let lastTs = null;
   332→
   333→    // Event log (newest-first)
   334→    const log = [];
   335→    const MAX_LOG = 150;
   336→    let logDirty = false;
   337→
   338→    // Track previous object states so we can log from→to
   339→    const prevStateMap = new Map();
   340→    for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   341→      prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   342→    }
   343→
   344→    // ── Controls ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   345→
   346→    const pauseBtn = document.getElementById('btn-pause');
   347→    pauseBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   348→      paused = !paused;
   349→      pauseBtn.innerHTML = paused ? '&#9654; Play' : '&#9646;&#9646; Pause';
   350→      pauseBtn.classList.toggle('active', paused);
   351→      if (!paused) lastTs = null; // avoid time-jump on resume
   352→    });
   353→
   354→    document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(btn => {
   355→      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   356→        speed = parseFloat(btn.dataset.speed);
   357→        document.querySelectorAll('.speed-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
   358→        btn.classList.add('active');
   359→      });
   360→    });
   361→
   362→    document.getElementById('btn-reset').addEventListener('click', () => {
   363→      // Reset object states and slot tracking to defaults
   364→      for (const def of OBJECT_DEFS) {
   365→        const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(def.id);
   366→        if (!obj) continue;
   367→        obj.state = def.state || 'idle';
   368→        obj._resetAutoTimer();
   369→        obj.clearSlots();
   370→        prevStateMap.set(def.id, obj.state);
   371→      }
   372→      // Reset sim clock
   373→      simEngine.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
   374→      // Clear log
   375→      log.length = 0;
   376→      logDirty = true;
   377→      // Update badge classes immediately
   378→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   379→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   380→      }
   381→    });
   382→
   383→    // ── Helper: state badge class ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   384→
   385→    const ACTIVE_STATES = new Set([
   386→      'cooking', 'brewing', 'painting', 'working', 'tending', 'reading', 'on',
   387→    ]);
   388→    const DONE_STATES = new Set(['done', 'ready', 'open', 'cozy', 'resting']);
   389→
   390→    function badgeClass(state) {
   391→      if (state === 'idle')         return 'idle';
   392→      if (DONE_STATES.has(state))   return 'done';
   393→      if (ACTIVE_STATES.has(state)) return 'active';
   394→      return 'other';
   395→    }
   396→
   397→    // ── Log helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   398→
   399→    function pushLog(objectId, fromState, toState, trigger) {
   400→      log.unshift({ objectId, fromState, toState, trigger, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   401→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   402→      logDirty = true;
   403→    }
   404→
   405→    function pushAILog(charLabel, action, target, dialogue) {
   406→      log.unshift({ type: 'ai', charLabel, action, target, dialogue, time: simEngine.getSimTimeString() });
   407→      if (log.length > MAX_LOG) log.length = MAX_LOG;
   408→      logDirty = true;
   409→    }
   410→
   411→    // ── Manual interact (called from interaction buttons) ─────────────────────
   412→
   413→    window._dbInteract = function(objectId, action) {
   414→      const obj = simEngine.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   415→      if (!obj) return;
   416→      const from = obj.state;
   417→      const ev = simEngine.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   418→      if (ev) {
   419→        pushLog(objectId, from, ev.state, action);
   420→        prevStateMap.set(objectId, ev.state);
   421→        updateObjectCard(obj);
   422→      }
   423→    };
   424→
   425→    // ── Build DOM cards (once) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
   426→
   427→    function initObjectCards() {
   428→      const grid = document.getElementById('objects-grid');
   429→      for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   430→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   431→        card.className = 'object-card';
   432→        card.id = `obj-${obj.id}`;
   433→        card.innerHTML = `
   434→          <div class="object-card-header">
   435→            <span class="object-name">${obj.name}</span>
   436→            <span class="state-badge" id="badge-${obj.id}"></span>
   437→          </div>
   438→          <div class="position-hint">tile (${obj.tx}, ${obj.ty})</div>
   439→          <div class="slot-info" id="slots-${obj.id}"></div>
   440→          <div class="timer-bar" id="timerbar-${obj.id}" style="display:none">
   441→            <div class="timer-fill" id="timerfill-${obj.id}" style="width:0%"></div>
   442→          </div>
   443→          <div class="timer-text" id="timertext-${obj.id}" style="display:none"></div>
   444→          <div class="interactions" id="int-${obj.id}"></div>
   445→        `;
   446→        grid.appendChild(card);
   447→        updateObjectCard(obj); // initial paint
   448→      }
   449→    }
   450→
   451→    function updateObjectCard(obj) {
   452→      const badge      = document.getElementById(`badge-${obj.id}`);
   453→      const timerBar   = document.getElementById(`timerbar-${obj.id}`);
   454→      const timerFill  = document.getElementById(`timerfill-${obj.id}`);
   455→      const timerText  = document.getElementById(`timertext-${obj.id}`);
   456→      const intDiv     = document.getElementById(`int-${obj.id}`);
   457→      if (!badge) return;
   458→
   459→      const prevState = badge.dataset.state;
   460→      const stateChanged = prevState !== obj.state;
   461→
   462→      if (stateChanged) {
   463→        badge.textContent = obj.state;
   464→        badge.className = `state-badge ${badgeClass(obj.state)}`;
   465→        badge.dataset.state = obj.state;
   466→
   467→        // Rebuild interaction buttons on state change
   468→        const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   469→        const actions = Object.keys(stateDef?.transitions || {});
   470→        intDiv.innerHTML = actions.map(a =>
   471→          `<button onclick="window._dbInteract('${obj.id}','${a}')">${a}</button>`
   472→        ).join('');
   473→      }
   474→
   475→      // Slot occupancy (update every frame)
   476→      const slotDiv = document.getElementById(`slots-${obj.id}`);
   477→      if (slotDiv) {
   478→        const si = obj.getSlotInfo();
   479→        const pips = [];
   480→        for (let i = 0; i < si.capacity; i++) {
   481→          let cls = 'available';
   482→          if (i < si.occupied)                      cls = 'occupied';
   483→          else if (i < si.occupied + si.reserved)   cls = 'reserved';
   484→          pips.push(`<div class="slot-pip ${cls}" title="${cls}"></div>`);
   485→        }
   486→        const labelCls = si.available === 0 ? 'slot-label full' : 'slot-label';
   487→        const labelTxt = si.available === 0 ? 'full' : `${si.available}/${si.capacity} free`;
   488→        slotDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="slot-pips">${pips.join('')}</div><span class="${labelCls}">${labelTxt}</span>`;
   489→      }
   490→
   491→      // Timer bar (update every frame regardless of state change)
   492→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   493→      const hasTimer = !!(stateDef?.auto_next && obj.autoTimer > 0);
   494→      if (hasTimer) {
   495→        const totalMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   496→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - obj.autoTimer / totalMs) * 100));
   497→        timerBar.style.display = '';
   498→        timerFill.style.width  = `${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
   499→        timerText.style.display = '';
   500→        timerText.textContent   = `${Math.ceil(obj.autoTimer / 1000)}s remaining`;
   501→      } else {
   502→        timerBar.style.display  = 'none';
   503→        timerText.style.display = 'none';
   504→      }
   505→    }
   506→
   507→    function initCharacterCards() {
   508→      const grid = document.getElementById('characters-grid');
   509→      simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => {
   510→        const card = document.createElement('div');
   511→        card.className = 'character-card';
   512→        card.id = `char-${i}`;
   513→        grid.appendChild(card);
   514→        updateCharacterCard(char, i); // initial paint
   515→      });
   516→    }
   517→
   518→    function updateCharacterCard(char, i) {
   519→      const card = document.getElementById(`char-${i}`);
   520→      if (!card) return;
   521→
   522→      const targetName = char.interactTarget
   523→        ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.interactTarget)?.name ?? char.interactTarget)
   524→        : char.targetObjectId
   525→          ? (simEngine.objectEngine.getById(char.targetObjectId)?.name ?? char.targetObjectId)
   526→          : '—';
   527→
   528→      // Hold countdown timer (shown while character is locked at an object)
   529→      let holdHtml = '';
   530→      if (char.action === 'interacting' && char.interactTimer > 0 && char.interactTimerMax > 0) {
   531→        const pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - char.interactTimer / char.interactTimerMax) * 100));
   532→        holdHtml = `
   533→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   534→            <span>Hold</span>
   535→            <span class="char-value">${Math.ceil(char.interactTimer / 1000)}s</span>
   536→          </div>
   537→          <div class="stat-bar">
   538→            <div class="stat-fill hold-timer" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   539→          </div>
   540→        `;
   541→      }
   542→
   543→      // AI decision cooldown timer
   544→      let cooldownHtml = '';
   545→      if (aiEngine.enabled) {
   546→        const remaining  = Math.max(0, aiEngine._timers.get(char.name) ?? aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs);
   547→        const pct        = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, (1 - remaining / aiEngine.decisionIntervalMs) * 100));
   548→        const secRemaining = Math.ceil(remaining / 1000);
   549→        cooldownHtml = `
   550→          <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   551→            <span>AI next</span>
   552→            <span class="char-value">${secRemaining}s</span>
   553→          </div>
   554→          <div class="stat-bar">
   555→            <div class="stat-fill ai-cooldown" style="width:${pct.toFixed(1)}%"></div>
   556→          </div>
   557→        `;
   558→      }
   559→
   560→      card.innerHTML = `
   561→        <div class="character-name">${char.label}</div>
   562→        <div class="char-row">
   563→          <span>Action</span>
   564→          <span class="action-badge ${char.action}">${char.action}</span>
   565→        </div>
   566→        <div class="char-row">
   567→          <span>Position</span>
   568→          <span class="char-value">(${Math.round(char.tx)}, ${Math.round(char.ty)})</span>
   569→        </div>
   570→        <div class="char-row">
   571→          <span>Facing</span>
   572→          <span class="char-value">${char.facing}</span>
   573→        </div>
   574→        <div class="char-row">
   575→          <span>Target</span>
   576→          <span class="char-value">${targetName}</span>
   577→        </div>
   578→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   579→          <span>Mood</span>
   580→          <span class="char-value">${char.mood}</span>
   581→        </div>
   582→        <div class="stat-bar">
   583→          <div class="stat-fill mood" style="width:${char.mood}%"></div>
   584→        </div>
   585→        <div class="char-row" style="margin-top:4px">
   586→          <span>Energy</span>
   587→          <span class="char-value">${char.energy}</span>
   588→        </div>
   589→        <div class="stat-bar">
   590→          <div class="stat-fill energy" style="width:${char.energy}%"></div>
   591→        </div>
   592→        ${holdHtml}
   593→        ${cooldownHtml}
   594→      `;
   595→    }
   596→
   597→    function renderEventLog() {
   598→      if (!logDirty) return;
   599→      logDirty = false;
   600→
   601→      const el = document.getElementById('event-log');
   602→      if (log.length === 0) {
   603→        el.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#555;padding:4px 0">No events yet.</div>';
   604→        return;
   605→      }
   606→      el.innerHTML = log.slice(0, 80).map(e => {
   607→        if (e.type === 'ai') {
   608→          const targetStr   = e.target   ? ` \u2192 ${e.target}` : '';
   609→          const dialogueStr = e.dialogue ? ` \u201c${e.dialogue}\u201d` : '';
   610→          return `
   611→            <div class="log-entry ai">
   612→              <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   613→              <span class="log-obj">${e.charLabel}</span>
   614→              <span class="log-transition">${e.action}${targetStr}${dialogueStr}</span>
   615→              <span class="log-tag ai">AI</span>
   616→            </div>
   617→          `;
   618→        }
   619→        return `
   620→          <div class="log-entry ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'interaction'}">
   621→            <span class="log-time">${e.time}</span>
   622→            <span class="log-obj">${e.objectId}</span>
   623→            <span class="log-transition">${e.fromState} &rarr; ${e.toState}</span>
   624→            <span class="log-tag ${e.trigger === 'auto' ? 'auto' : 'use'}">${e.trigger}</span>
   625→          </div>
   626→        `;
   627→      }).join('');
   628→    }
   629→
   630→    // ── Tick loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   631→
   632→    function tick(ts) {
   633→      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   634→
   635→      if (!paused && lastTs !== null) {
   636→        const realDelta = (ts - lastTs) * speed;
   637→
   638→        // Snapshot states before update
   639→        const snap = new Map();
   640→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) snap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   641→
   642→        // Advance simulation
   643→        simEngine.update(realDelta);
   644→
   645→        // Detect auto-transitions
   646→        for (const obj of simEngine.objectEngine.getAll()) {
   647→          if (snap.get(obj.id) !== obj.state) {
   648→            pushLog(obj.id, snap.get(obj.id), obj.state, 'auto');
   649→            prevStateMap.set(obj.id, obj.state);
   650→          }
   651→          updateObjectCard(obj);
   652→        }
   653→
   654→        // Update character cards
   655→        simEngine.characters.forEach((char, i) => updateCharacterCard(char, i));
   656→      }
   657→
   658→      lastTs = ts;
   659→
   660→      // Clock
   661→      document.getElementById('clock').textContent = simEngine.getSimTimeString();
   662→
   663→      // Event log (only when dirty)
   664→      renderEventLog();
   665→    }
   666→
   667→    // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   668→
   669→    initObjectCards();
   670→    initCharacterCards();
   671→    requestAnimationFrame(tick);
   672→  </script>
   673→</body>
   674→</html>
   675→

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #25
Now I have a thorough understanding of the codebase. Let me understand the issue and plan the implementation. ## Issue FRG-223: Agent-to-Agent Handshaking (Talk Protocol) ### Current Problem Talk is fire-and-forget: Character A decides to talk to B, walks over, and speaks — regardless of B's state. B could be sleeping, interacting with an object, or already talking to someone else. ### Requirements 1. **Request Phase:** When A decides to talk to B, A sends an interaction request. 2. **Evaluate Phase:** B checks current priority/state: * If idle or walking → Accept * If sleeping, interacting, or already in conversation → Reject 3. **Synchronization:** If accepted, both enter a shared 'talking' state. Both face each other. Individual AI decision timers pause until conversation ends. 4. **Conversation Duration:** Configurable (e.g., 10-15s), then both return to idle. 5. **Rejection Handling:** If B rejects, A falls back to alternative action (see fallback ticket). ### Acceptance Criteria Characters won't initiate conversations with unavailable targets, both will visibly synchronize their states and pause decision-making during the exchange, and the debug interface will track active conversation pairs and their status. ### Current Talk Implementation The existing `talk` case in `AIEngine.js` is fire-and-forget—it walks character A toward B and displays speech bubbles without actually checking if B is available or putting either character into a proper conversation state. The AI timers keep running, there's no synchronization between the two characters, and there's no way to handle rejection. ### My Plan I need to add a `'talking'` state to the character's action states and introduce `talkTimer` and `talkTimerMax` fields to manage conversation duration. I'll also add a `talkTarget` field to track who each character is talking to. During the `update()` method, when a character is talking, their timer counts down until the conversation ends and they return to idle. Importantly, I need to prevent the `wanderTimer` from ticking while a character is either talking or interacting, and extend the AI timer pause logic in `AIEngine.update()` to include the `'talking'` state alongside `'interacting'`. Then I'll add a `startConversation()` method to the `SimulationEngine` that gets called once character A reaches B's adjacent tile, establishing the handshake between both characters. For the AI logic, I need to check whether the target character can actually accept a conversation—they should only accept if they're idle or walking, otherwise the request gets rejected and A falls back to idle. The `'talking'` state also needs to be added to the list where AI timers don't fire. Finally, I'll update the debug display to show the talking action badge, the conversation partner in the target field, and the remaining hold timer. Now I'm thinking through the actual flow: AI decides to talk to character B, and before walking there... When A arrives at B's location, both characters enter the talking state with matching timers and face each other. While they're talking, the wander timer freezes and AI timers don't execute. Once the timer expires, they both return to idle. The challenge is detecting when A has actually arrived at the adjacent tile—that happens in the Engine's update loop. I need to mirror the existing object arrival pattern: when a character has a `talkTargetCharacter` reference set and reaches idle state, I'll trigger a talk arrival handler that verifies B is still available before initiating the conversation. For the facing logic, I'm calculating the direction vector between the two characters and setting their facing directions so they look at each other based on which axis has the larger distance. Now I need to pause the decision timer when a character is in talking state, not just interacting, so they don't interrupt conversations. I also need to add `talking` as a valid action state and create the necessary fields like `talkTimer` and `talkTarget` to track conversation state. For the engine, I'm handling the arrival logic when a character reaches their talk target, then triggering the actual conversation start. The AIEngine needs to validate that the target character can accept the conversation request, set up the target reference, and manage when to actually begin the dialogue — either immediately or once both characters are ready. I should also log if a character rejects the talk request because they're busy. On the debug page, I want to display the talking state with its own badge style, show who each character is talking to, display the conversation timer while it's active, and make rejected talk attempts visually distinct in the logs. Now I'm setting up the Character class with the necessary fields for managing conversations — the action state, a timer for tracking how long the conversation lasts, and references to the target character. I'm debating the naming convention for these properties to keep them consistent and clear. I'll use `pendingTalkTarget` for the character someone is walking toward (set by the AI engine), and `talkTarget` for the actual conversation partner once both characters are in the talking state. In the update loop, when the talk timer expires, I'll reset the action back to idle, clear the target, and restart the wander timer. I need to make sure the wander timer doesn't decrement while already in idle state... Actually, looking at the code flow, the wander timer only decrements in the idle branch, so it's already protected during talking. For the engine, I need to check for talk arrival before checking if it's time to wander, so characters transition into conversation before potentially wandering off.    163→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   164→
   165→  get px() {
   166→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   167→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   168→    }
   169→    const next = this.path[0];
   170→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   171→  }
   172→
   173→  get py() {
   174→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   175→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   176→    }
   177→    const next = this.path[0];
   178→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   179→  }

   105→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

   107→  /**
   108→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   109→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   110→   */
   111→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   112→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   113→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, char.pendingAction || 'use');
   114→
   115→    if (event) {
   116→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   117→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   118→
   119→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   120→
   121→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   122→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   123→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   124→      if (obj && event.state) {
   125→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   126→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   127→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   128→        }
   129→      }
   130→
   131→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs);
   132→
   133→      if (event.speech) {
   134→        char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   135→      }
   136→
   137→      if (event.emoji) {
   138→        this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   139→      }
   140→    } else {
   141→      // No valid transition — release the reservation
   142→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   143→    }
   144→    // Always clear targeting so we don't re-fire on next idle frame
   145→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   146→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   147→  }
   148→
   149→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   150→
   151→  /**
   152→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   153→   * Re-evaluates B's availability; starts conversation or logs rejection.
   154→   */
   155→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   156→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   157→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   158→
   159→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   160→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';

   169→      return;
   170→    }
   171→

   174→
   175→  /**
   176→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   177→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   178→   */
   179→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   180→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   181→  }
   182→
   183→  /**
   184→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   185→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   186→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   187→   */
   188→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   189→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   190→
   191→    // Face each other
   192→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   193→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   194→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   195→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   196→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   197→    } else {
   198→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   199→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   200→    }
   201→
   202→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles
   203→    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {
   204→      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;
   205→      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;
   206→    }
   207→    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {
   208→      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;
   209→      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);
   213→    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);
   214→
   215→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   216→      type:           'conversation_start',
   217→      initiatorLabel: charA.label,
   218→      targetLabel:    charB.label,
   219→    });
   220→  }
   221→
   222→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   223→
   224→  _doWander(char) {
   225→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   226→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   227→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   228→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   229→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   230→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   231→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   232→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   233→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);

   244→  update(deltaMs) {
   245→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   246→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   247→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   248→
   249→      // Update facing toward next tile in path

   253→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   254→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   255→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   256→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   257→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   258→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   259→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   260→      }
   261→
   262→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   263→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   264→        this.action       = 'idle';
   265→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   266→        this._playAnim('idle');
   267→      } else {
   268→        this._playWalkAnim();
   269→      }

   272→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #98
Looks good. Now let me also look at what happens when Engine update is checking for the `'idle'` condition with `pendingTalkTarget`. There's a potential issue: when A has been walking to B's location with `pendingTalkTarget` set, and A arrives (action becomes `'idle'`), `_handleTalkArrival` is called. But there's also `_handleObjectArrival` check. Let me make sure these don't conflict. Looking at the code: ```js // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) { this._handleObjectArrival(char); } // Handle arrival: character reached talk target if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) { this._handleTalkArrival(char); } ``` If both `targetObjectId` and `pendingTalkTarget` are set simultaneously (which shouldn't happen since they're mutually exclusive), the object arrival handler runs first, but then `startTalk` clears `targetObjectId` anyway, so there's no actual conflict. Actually, I need to reconsider the order here. When `_handleTalkArrival` runs and calls `startTalk`, it clears `targetObjectId` — but `_handleObjectArrival` already executed before that point, so the clearing happens after. The real question is whether `targetObjectId` can even be set while `pendingTalkTarget` is active. Looking at the `talk` decision in AIEngine, it doesn't clear `targetObjectId`, so I should verify if that's actually a problem. Looking at the `talk` case in AIEngine, I notice I'm not clearing `targetObjectId` when a character decides to talk to another character. In the `interact` case, this gets properly released when switching targets, but the `talk` case skips this step. This creates a bug where if a character is already walking to an object and then the AI decides to talk instead, both `targetObjectId` and `pendingTalkTarget` end up set, causing both arrival handlers to potentially fire. I need to add the same object reservation cleanup that `move` and `interact` cases already do.

llm.js
/**
 * /api/llm — Vercel serverless proxy for OpenRouter LLM calls.
 * Keeps the API key server-side. The client sends the same Anthropic-style
 * messages payload; we forward it to OpenRouter and relay the response.
 */

export default async function handler(req, res) {
  // CORS headers for same-origin fetch from the static frontend
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'POST, OPTIONS');
  res.setHeader('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type');

  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return res.status(200).end();
  }

  if (req.method !== 'POST') {
    return res.status(405).json({ error: 'Method not allowed' });
  }

// B is busy now\n\nconst charC = new Character({ name: 'Ash', label: 'Nyx', tx: 3, ty: 5, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });\nengine.addCharacter(charC);\nengine.pendingEvents.length = 0; // clear\n\ncharC.pendingTalkTarget = charB;\nengine._handleTalkArrival(charC);\n\nconsole.assert(charC.action === 'idle', `charC should stay idle, got ${charC.action}`);\nconsole.assert(charB.action === 'interacting', 'charB should still be interacting');\nconsole.assert(engine.pendingEvents.some(e => e.type === 'talk_rejected'), 'talk_rejected event should be pushed');\n\nconsole.log('Rejection test passed!');\nconsole.log('All Engine tests passed!');\nEOF"

= Array.from({ length: GRID_ROWS }, (_, row) =>\n  Array.from({ length: GRID_COLS }, (_, col) =>\n    col >= 1 && col <= 17 && row >= 2 && row <= 9\n  )\n);\n\nconst engine = new AIEngine({ endpoint: null }); // disabled\n\nconst charA = new Character({ name: 'Amelia', label: 'Maple', tx: 5, ty: 5, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });\nconst charB = new Character({ name: 'Lucy', label: 'Sol', tx: 7, ty: 5, walkable, gridCols: GRID_COLS, gridRows: GRID_ROWS });\n\nconst events = [];\nconst simState = {\n  timeString: '10:00 AM',\n  findAdjacentWalkable: (tx, ty) => {\n    const dirs = [{ tx, ty: ty - 1 }, { tx, ty: ty + 1 }, { tx: tx - 1, ty }, { tx: tx + 1, ty }];\n    return dirs.find(d => walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) ?? null;\n  },\n  pushEvent: (ev) => events.push(ev),\n};\n\n// Test 1: talk to idle charB \u2014 should succeed (set pendingTalkTarget)\nengine._applyDecision(charA, {\n  action: 'talk',\n  targetCharacter: 'Sol',\n  dialogue: 'Hey Sol!',\n  targetDialogue: 'Hey Maple!',\n}, [charA, charB], [], simState);\n\nconsole.assert(charA.pendingTalkTarget === charB, `pendingTalkTarget should be charB, got ${charA.pendingTalkTarget}`);\nconsole.assert(charA.action === 'walking', `charA should be walking, got ${charA.action}`);\nconsole.assert(charA.pendingTalkDialogue === 'Hey Sol!', 'dialogue stored');\nconsole.assert(charA.pendingTalkResponse === 'Hey Maple!', 'response stored');\nconsole.assert(events.length === 0, 'no rejection events for accepted talk');\nconsole.log('Talk accepted test passed!');\n\n// Reset\ncharA.path = [];\ncharA.action = 'idle';\ncharA.pendingTalkTarget = null;\nevents.length = 0;\n\n// Test 2: talk to busy charB \u2014 should reject\ncharB.action = 'interacting';\nengine._applyDecision(charA, {\n  action: 'talk',\n  targetCharacter: 'Sol',\n  dialogue: 'Hey Sol!',\n}, [charA, charB], [], simState);\n\nconsole.assert(charA.pendingTalkTarget === null, 'no pendingTalkTarget when rejected');\nconsole.assert(charA.action === 'idle', `charA stays idle when rejected, got ${charA.action}`);\nconsole.assert(events.some(e => e.type === 'talk_rejected'), 'talk_rejected pushed to events');\nconsole.log('Talk rejected test passed!');\n\n// Test 3: timer pauses during talking\nconst ai2 = new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'http://fake', decisionIntervalMs: 5000 });\ncharA.action = 'talking';\nai2._timers.set(charA.name, -100); // timer expired\nlet decideCalled = false;\nai2._requestDecision = () => { decideCalled = true; };\nai2.update(100, [charA], [], simState);\nconsole.assert(!decideCalled, 'AI decision should NOT fire while talking');\ncharA.action = 'idle';\nai2.update(100, [charA], [], simState);\nconsole.assert(decideCalled, 'AI decision SHOULD fire when idle');\nconsole.log('AI timer pause test passed!');\n\nconsole.log('All AIEngine tests passed!');\nEOF"

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #122
Bash TOOL CALL 
{
  "command": "gh pr create --title \"feat: agent-to-agent handshaking talk protocol (FRG-223)\" --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\n## Summary\n\n- Replaces fire-and-forget talk with a full request/evaluate/synchronise protocol\n- Characters now check if the target is available before initiating a conversation; if the target is `interacting` or already `talking`, the request is rejected immediately and logged\n- On arrival, the engine re-validates the target's state (graceful rejection if target became busy during the walk)\n- Both characters enter a shared `talking` state: they face each other, AI timers pause, and speech bubbles fire at conversation start\n- Conversation lasts 10\u201315 s (random), then both return to `idle`\n- Debug page updated: `talking` action badge, conversation partner shown in Target row, hold-timer bar, and TALK/REJECT entries in the event log\n\n## Acceptance Criteria Coverage\n\n- \u2705 Characters don't talk to sleeping/busy characters (evaluate phase + arrival re-check)\n- \u2705 Both characters visibly enter conversation state (`talking` action badge, face each other)\n- \u2705 Decision timers pause during conversation (`char.action !== 'talking'` guard in AIEngine)\n- \u2705 Debug page shows conversation pairs and state (Target row + TALK log entry)\n- \u2705 Rejected talk attempts logged in event log (REJECT log entry)\n\n## Key Decisions\n\n- **No hard \"reservation\" of B**: target availability is checked at decision time and re-checked on arrival. If B becomes busy in between, A falls back gracefully. Simpler than a reservation system and sufficient for the use case.\n- **No `sleeping` state yet**: the codebase has no sleep state; rejection covers `interacting` and `talking`. Sleep can be added later without changing this protocol.\n- **Dialogue held until arrival**: `pendingTalkDialogue`/`pendingTalkResponse` are stored on the initiator and transferred to `pendingSpeech` only when the conversation actually starts, so speech bubbles are truthful.\n\n## Test plan\n\n- [ ] Run debug.html with AI enabled and observe TALK events in the event log\n- [ ] Verify that characters who are `interacting` receive REJECT events when targeted\n- [ ] Verify `talking` badge appears on both characters and both face each other\n- [ ] Verify the hold-timer bar counts down during conversation (~10\u201315 s)\n- [ ] Verify AI decisions don't fire for characters while `action === 'talking'`\n\n\ud83e\udd16 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\""
}

{"id":"a1731020-a00c-42a0-bca9-35da9eeb8748","identifier":"FRG-223","title":"Agent-to-Agent Handshaking (Talk Protocol)","description":"Character-to-character interaction needs a request/response protocol instead of forced interaction.

## Current Problem

Talk is fire-and-forget: Character A decides to talk to B, walks over, and speaks — regardless of B's state. B could be sleeping, interacting with an object, or already talking to someone else.

## Requirements

1. **Request Phase:** When A decides to talk to B, A sends an interaction request.
2. **Evaluate Phase:** B checks current priority/state:
   * If idle or walking → Accept
   * If sleeping, interacting, or already in conversation → Reject
3. **Synchronization:** If accepted, both enter a shared 'talking' state. Both face each other. Individual AI decision timers pause until conversation ends.
4. **Conversation Duration:** Configurable (e.g., 10-15s), then both return to idle.
5. **Rejection Handling:** If B rejects, A falls back to alternative action (see fallback ticket).

## Acceptance Criteria

* Characters don't talk to sleeping/busy characters
* Both characters visibly enter conversation state
* Decision timers pause during conversation
* Debug page shows conversation pairs and state

## Status DONE ## What Changed - `src/Character.js` — Added `talking` state to comment; added `talkTimer`, `talkTimerMax`, `talkTarget`, `pendingTalkTarget`, `pendingTalkDialogue`, `pendingTalkResponse` fields; added `startTalk()` method; added `talking` branch in `update()` that ticks timer and returns to idle on expiry - `src/Engine.js` — Added `pendingTalkTarget` arrival check in `update()`; added `_handleTalkArrival()` (re-evaluates B's availability, logs rejection or starts conversation); added `_startConversation()` (faces both characters toward each other, transfers queued dialogue to speech bubbles, calls `startTalk()` on both, pushes `conversation_start` event) - `src/AIEngine.js` — Added `char.action !== 'talking'` guard so AI timers pause during conversations; rewrote `talk` case to check target availability upfront (reject → push `talk_rejected` event + set A idle; accept → release previous object reservation and set `pendingTalkTarget`); skipped premature `currentDialogue` assignment for `talk` actions - `debug.html` — Added `.action-badge.talking` CSS; `.log-entry.talk`/`.log-entry.reject` log styles; updated `updateCharacterCard()` to show conversation partner in Target row and hold-timer during `talking`; added `conversation_start`/`talk_rejected` rendering in `renderEventLog()`; added `pendingEvents` consumption loop in tick ## Key Decisions - No hard reservation of B: availability checked at decision time and re-checked on arrival — simpler than a slot reservation, sufficient for the use case - No `sleeping` state yet: codebase has none; rejection covers `interacting` and `talking` - Dialogue speech bubbles fire at conversation start (on arrival), not at decision time ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-223-agent-to-agent-handshaking` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/9
